\section{CONSUMER}

\subsection{Optimisation problem}

\begin{align}
&\max_{\left({D}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{d}}\rangle}\right)_{{i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{d}}\in {P\!c\!o\!n}}
} U = \left(\sum_{{i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{c}}\in {P\!c\!o\!n}} {{\alpha}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{c}}\rangle}} {{{D}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{c}}\rangle}}^{{\omega}^{-1} \left(-1 + \omega\right)}}\right)^{{\omega} \left(-1 + \omega\right)^{-1}}\\
&\mathrm{s.t.:}\nonumber\\
& {C\!S} + {S\!A\!V} + \sum_{{i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{i}^{\mathrm{1}}}\in {P\!c\!o\!n}} {{p}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{i}^{\mathrm{1}}}\rangle}} {{D}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{i}^{\mathrm{1}}}\rangle}} = {I\!N\!C} \quad \left(\lambda^{\mathrm{CONSUMER}^{\mathrm{1}}}\right)
\end{align}


\subsection{Identities}

\begin{equation}
{I\!N\!C} = {B\!T\!I\!N\!C} - {P\!I\!T\!A\!X}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
{B\!T\!I\!N\!C} = {f\!a\!c\!t}^{\mathrm{row}^{\in^{\mathrm{k}^{\mathrm{data}}}}} + {f\!a\!c\!t}^{\mathrm{row}^{\in^{\mathrm{l}^{\mathrm{data}}}}} + {P\!S\!h} + {T\!R\!G\!O\!V} + {T\!R\!E\!M\!P} + {{p\!k}} {{K\!h}} + {w} {{L\!h}}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
{S\!A\!V} = {{p\!o\!r}^{\mathrm{sav}}} {{I\!N\!C}}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
{C\!S} = {{p\!o\!r}^{\mathrm{cont}}} {{I\!N\!C}}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
{D}^{\langle \mathrm{prod}^{\mathrm{Min}}\rangle} = {{d\!s\!t}^{\mathrm{nc}}}^{\langle \mathrm{\mathrm{prod}^{\mathrm{Min}}}\rangle}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
{D}^{\langle \mathrm{prod}^{\mathrm{const}}\rangle} = {{d\!s\!t}^{\mathrm{nc}}}^{\langle \mathrm{\mathrm{prod}^{\mathrm{const}}}\rangle}
\end{equation}


\subsection{First order conditions}

\begin{equation}
{i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{d}}\in {P\!c\!o\!n}\colon\quad -{\lambda^{\mathrm{CONSUMER}^{\mathrm{1}}}} {{p}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{d}}\rangle}} + {{\alpha}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{d}}\rangle}} {{{D}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{d}}\rangle}}^{-1 + {\omega}^{-1} \left(-1 + \omega\right)}} {\left(\sum_{{i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{c}}\in {P\!c\!o\!n}} {{\alpha}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{c}}\rangle}} {{{D}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{c}}\rangle}}^{{\omega}^{-1} \left(-1 + \omega\right)}}\right)^{-1 + {\omega} \left(-1 + \omega\right)^{-1}}} = 0
 \quad \left({D}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{d}}\rangle}\right)
\end{equation}

\begin{equation}
-w + {{{b\!e\!t\!a\!l}}^{\langle {s\!c}\rangle}} {{\gamma}^{\langle {s\!c}\rangle}} \left(\left(1 - {{t\!e\!s}}^{\langle {s\!c}\rangle} - {{t\!p\!s}}^{\langle {s\!c}\rangle}\right) \left(\sum_{{i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{pv}}\in P} {{{m\!a\!k\!e}^{\mathrm{share}}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{pv}},{s\!c}\rangle}} {{{p\!z}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{pv}}\rangle}}\right) - \sum_{{i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{x}^{\mathrm{o}}}\in {P\!n\!o\!5}} {{{i\!o}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{x}^{\mathrm{o}}},{s\!c}\rangle}} {{p}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{x}^{\mathrm{o}}}\rangle}}\right) {{{K}^{\langle {s\!c}\rangle}}^{{{b\!e\!t\!a\!k}}^{\langle {s\!c}\rangle}}} {{{L}^{\langle {s\!c}\rangle}}^{-1 + {{b\!e\!t\!a\!l}}^{\langle {s\!c}\rangle}}} = 0
 \quad \left({L}^{\langle {s\!c}\rangle}\right)
\end{equation}




\section{EXPORTER ${i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\in P^{\mathrm{Exp}}$}

\subsection{Optimisation problem}

\begin{align}
&\max_{{Z}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}, {{D\!S}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}, {{E\!X}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}
} {\Pi^{\mathrm{CET}}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle} = {{{p\!d}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}} {{{D\!S}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}} + {{{p\!e}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}} {{{E\!X}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}} - {{{p\!z}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}} {{Z}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}}\\

\begin{equation}

 \quad \left({Z}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}\right)

\begin{equation}

 \quad \left({{D\!S}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}\right)
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
{{p\!e}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle} + {{{a\!t}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}} {{\gamma^{\mathrm{e}}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}} {{\lambda^{\mathrm{EXPORTER}^{\mathrm{1}}}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}} {{{{E\!X}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}}^{-1 + {\sigma^{\mathrm{t}}}^{-1} \left(1 + \sigma^{\mathrm{t}}\right)}} {\left({{\gamma^{\mathrm{e}}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}} {{{{E\!X}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}}^{{\sigma^{\mathrm{t}}}^{-1} \left(1 + \sigma^{\mathrm{t}}\right)}} + \left(1 - {\gamma^{\mathrm{e}}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}\right) {{{{D\!S}}^{\langle {i\!d\!x}^{\mathrm{e}}\rangle}}^{{\sigma^{\mathrm{t}}}^{-1} \left(1 + \sigma^{\mathrm{t}}\right)}}\right)^{-1 + {\sigma^{\mathrm{t}}} \left(1 + \sigma^{\mathrm{t}}\right)^{-1}}} = 0

\begin{equation}
